  holdtime 600

  link-delay-down 200

$

interface xgei-0/1/0/2

  holdtime 600

$

interface xgei-0/1/0/3

  port-alarm sd-fer enable

  port-alarm sd-fer occur coefficient 1 exponent 6 clear coefficient 1 exponent 

6 period 20

  sd-detection times 1

$

interface cgei-0/3/0/1

  link-delay-down 200

  link-delay-up 2000

$

interface cgei-0/4/0/1

  link-delay-down 200

  link-delay-up 2000

$

interface xgei-0/6/0/1

  holdtime 600

$

interface xgei-0/6/1/5

  holdtime 600

  link-delay-down 200

$

!</port-physical-config>
